\DoxyCodeLine{00755\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ asymmetrical\ results\ on\ the\ raster\ grid.\ Therefore\ we're\ rounding\ N\ to\ next\ even\ number\ (7-\/>8,\ 8-\/>8,\ 9-\/>10\ etc.)}}
